MANUALLY VERIFIED — 5 TRUE NEGATIVES (correctly NOT emitted as edges)
================================================================================

TRUE NEGATIVE 1: app/models/account.rb:363 — `rescue ActiveRecord::RecordInvalid => e`
  `ActiveRecord::RecordInvalid` correctly skipped because the FQCN starts
  with the prefix `ActiveRecord::` (STOP_PREFIXES). It's a framework
  exception class, not a project file.

TRUE NEGATIVE 2: app/models/account.rb:253 — `"#{username}@#{Rails.configuration.x.local_domain}"`
  `Rails` correctly skipped — top-level stoplisted (STOP_TOP_LEVEL). No
  app/rails.rb edge attempted. Same treatment for `Rails.cache.fetch(...)` at
  account.rb:397, 401.

TRUE NEGATIVE 3: app/lib/emoji_formatter.rb:14 — `# @option options [String] :style`
  `String` (Ruby builtin) is stoplisted at the top level. Even though this
  is inside a comment (and our AST walk would not visit it anyway), if a
  real String reference appeared elsewhere, it would correctly produce no
  edge. Confirmed by absence of any `app/lib/string.rb` candidate and
  no edge emitted for `String` anywhere in the output.

TRUE NEGATIVE 4: app/controllers/auth/sessions_controller.rb:3 — `class Auth::SessionsController < Devise::SessionsController`
  `Devise::SessionsController` correctly skipped — prefix `Devise::` is in
  STOP_PREFIXES. Mastodon depends on the Devise gem but vendors no Devise
  file, so emitting an edge would be meaningless. (Note: this leaves
  Devise-derived controllers with no superclass edge — a known limitation,
  acceptable because gem sources are not in the index.)

TRUE NEGATIVE 5: Across all parsed files, the constants `Hash`, `Array`,
  `Symbol`, `Integer`, `Time`, `JSON`, `URI`, `Encoding`, `Process`,
  `Concern` (ActiveSupport::Concern), `StandardError`, `RuntimeError`,
  `NilClass`, `TrueClass`, `FalseClass`, `Errno::*`, `Math::*` — none of
  these produced any edge in the 2809 emitted. Verified by grep over
  poc-output.raw.txt:
     $ grep -E "constant '(Hash|Array|String|Integer|Time|JSON)'" poc-output.raw.txt
     (no matches)

================================================================================
OBSERVATIONS / NOTES
================================================================================

- The first edge for many controllers is `ApplicationController` (line 3),
  hitting the per-app override of the stoplist. That's the desired behaviour.
- Render edges resolve well; the simple regex pass over view files
  (.erb/.haml) catches partials referenced from views without needing a
  full template parser.
- No false positives surfaced in the spot-check of the first 40 edges —
  but only 10 were manually deep-verified. Long-tail false-positive rate
  unknown; see spec.md §6 "Risks".
